window.onerror = function onErrorFunc(msg, url, line, colno, error) {
if(!window.ta || !ta.has('ta.js_error_array.processed')) {
if(typeof js_error_array == 'undefined') {
js_error_array = [];
}
var err = error;
js_error_array[js_error_array.length] = {'msg': msg, 'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'error': err, 'ready_state': document.readyState};
return true;
}
else {
if(window.ta && ta.util && ta.util.error && ta.util.error.record) {
ta.util.error.record(error, 'error post load:: ' + msg, null, {'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'ready_state': document.readyState});
}
}
};
</script>

           <div class="modules-membercenter-about-me " data-ox-name="modules.membercenter.AboutMe" data-ox-context="MemberCenter_ProfileData, Errors, Member"> 
            <div class="aboutMe profileBox">
             <span class="header">About Me</span> 
             <div class="info">
              <p>Since Dec 2006</p>
              <p>Lives in Western Cape, South Africa</p>
              <p> 65+ year old male </p>
              <p>May I tell you a little about what I do? Please start here: https://vimeo.com/103647546 I am a lucky American, living on the oceanfront about 100 miles east of Cape Town several months each year - the rest of the time just outside Phoenix, Arizona USA. I operate a safari business with important priorities: Emphasis on personal attention - Discounts - Value for money. If you are planning a safari I would be pleased to tell you about discounted rates that will help your budget. I am a specialist in the Sabi Sand reserve, and also send guests to many of the fine lodges &amp; camps in the rest of South Africa and Botswana. I handle custom safaris for individuals, couples &amp; families, groups of any size. If you would like to discuss a trip with me, please email me: dave@theafricasafari.com Web site is www.theafricasafari.com - nothing spectacular - just a simple explanation of my philosophy. </p>
             </div>
            </div>
